10-25-2023 16-17-40 Ben Sontag Hey pledges! You may have already seen/looked into it but next term we need someone to run for interim House Manager. We’d love to let this be a chance to get a 26 to step into Sig Nu leadership. Additionally, if any 26s were thinking about running for full year House Manager starting in the spring, acting first as interim House Manager will allow you a great chance to learn the ropes and test the waters before jumping in. So here I’ll give some brief info on what the job entails.
10-25-2023 16-17-54 Ben Sontag The job of the House Manager is safety and maintenance. This means fixing broken items/furniture/fixtures/appliances or taking the initiative to speak to professionals who know how. This means ensuring that the house stays up to code, and that it is fire safe. In my opinion it’s a very fun and rewarding job, getting to go to Home Depot and fix what needs to be fixed to make sure the house stays up and running.
